ALL 50 U.S. STATES AND THEIR CITIES / INCORPORATED PLACES
U.S. Census Bureau Vintage 2025 incorporated-place series
District of Columbia excluded; 19,482 place records total.
Includes cities, towns, villages, boroughs, municipalities, and equivalent incorporated governments.
Source: https://www2.census.gov/programs-surveys/popest/datasets/2020-2025/cities/totals/sub-est2025.csv
